				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Fantasia and Fugue in G minor, BWV 542 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1867 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Fantasias&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Fantasias</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Fugues&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Fugues</a></span>; <td>Based on the Bach-Gesellschaft Ausgabe, without the pitches in parentheses<br />Violins I, II, Violas, Cellos I, II-Contrabass.
